Speeches by Important Figures 108

Chairman Dai Jitao's Opening Address

Forge a Solid Physique

Cultivate a Strong Spirit

Chairman Dai Jitao said in his speech: "Only with a sound body can we have a sound mind. Only with sound citizens can we form a sound nation. And only with a sound nation can we create a sound culture. Looking at the past and present, spanning the universe, there has never been a case where a nation was weak and enervated, yet its culture could flourish and expand, or its nation could maintain its independence and survival. Before the revolution was complete and the nation was just beginning to be built, the central government deeply considered the lack of vigor in national physical education, which is the root cause of cultural decline and a means of inviting insults and causing chaos. Wishing to fundamentally change customs and establish a new foundation, it resolutely decided to hold a national sports meet. The site was selected in Hangzhou in April, and preparations were carried out for more than half a year. The sports-minded people of the country were delighted and danced with joy upon hearing the news, and they gathered to witness its completion. Various provinces and cities across the country selected and recommended outstanding talents who enthusiastically came to the meeting. From Hebei and Liaoning in the north to the Lingnan region in the south, and as far as the descendants of the Chinese nation overseas, more than 2,000 people will participate. The time is the transition between spring and warmth, a time when all things germinate. The location is Goujian's [of Yue] place of gathering and breeding, and Wu Su [of Wuyue] defended this place with self-improvement. It is a moment of vigorous striving that has lasted for a thousand years. Since the decline of military virtue, this is the first time that the entire country has gathered for a general competition. In ancient Athens, there was the Olympic Games. In our nation's golden age, there was also the system of hunting and military training. The people were accustomed to hard work, and their spirit soared to the heavens. The atmosphere of national revival was naturally different from that of later generations. With the decline of culture, physical strength gradually disappeared, and the physical body became thinner and weaker. This led to the deterioration of the people's morals, the darkening of the people's intellect, and the exhaustion of the people's livelihood, to the point where it could not be saved. Even selecting and nurturing seedlings and breeding species still requires artificial selection. How can we say that preserving the race and protecting the group does not require efforts to transform natural selection? Moreover, in modern physical education, concepts are constantly renewed, methods are constantly advanced, and regulations are detailed and meticulous. Every movement must be on course, which is how the laws of life are cultivated. The slightest deviation is fleeting. Superb skills are accumulated over time, so agility, diligence, and perseverance are essential. The loss of one person may mislead the group. One wrong action may affect the whole situation. This is how teamwork is practiced. Its effectiveness is not limited to increasing physical strength and improving the body. It will directly overcome the heavens and save the world. Sun Yat-sen said that modern warfare always sees weak countries as a problem, so peaceful nations need self-defense even more. If the mythical creatures qilin and wenhui had claws and teeth, how could eagles and tigers succeed? Our party upholds his teachings and firmly believes in his principles, which are to seek equality for the country and to achieve universal harmony in the world. It is especially important to develop national physical education as the foundation of the great cause of nation-building. I hope that from now on, this meeting will be held every year in different locations. The reputation it creates will spread from cities to villages, from schools to society, so that every household will make physical education a regular part of their lives, forging a solid physique and cultivating a strong spirit. Freedom from illness is true freedom. Fearlessness of the strong is true equality. A strong father will never have a weak son. Eugenics are the way to improve the breed. Then the nation will be healthy and strong, and the foundation of the country will be solid. Competition rules will become customs. Be upright, not deceitful. Compete without conflict. Protect what should be protected in terms of rights, and fulfill all obligations. The powerful and the inferior will not be able to deceive, and cunning and luck will be disdained. Then autonomy will have a solid foundation, and the rights of the people will be asserted. Those with full muscles will be diligent. Those with joyful spirits will enjoy their work. Do not seize what is not yours, and do not take what is unjust. Then the economy will be prosperous, and the people's livelihood will be secure. It is known that the governance of the country depends on the prosperity and decline of society. The prosperity and decline of society depends on the vigor and decline of the people's hearts. And the development of physical education is essential to stimulating the people's hearts and promoting the people's aspirations. This association has been ordered by the central government to gather these talented people, each displaying their unique talents, jointly setting a good example. I firmly believe that the future of physical education in our country will advance by leaps and bounds. The wind is bright, the banners are fluttering. Mount Wu stands tall, and West Lake is beautiful. Remembering the vastness of the rivers and mountains, we wish the country's fortune will be limitless. People of the whole country, why not come?"

Vice Chairman Zhang's Welcome Address 109

Celebrate Boundless Progress

Vice Chairman Zhang Renjie delivered the welcome speech on behalf of Shi Weihuan: "The lake and mountains are warm in spring, and events are starting in this broad space. Distinguished guests have come to a magnificent gathering. Knowledge is imparted, skills are assessed, rewards are given generously, and national practices are demonstrated. Talents of the time are each giving their best. Kunwu [a sword] shines brightly, and Ganjiang [another sword] soars into the sky. Spirits are invigorated, and ambitions are raised. Success is achieved, preserving the race and strengthening the nation. I am untalented, bearing responsibility for my hometown. As the host, I have the honor of assisting in the affairs of the meeting. Many talented people have come, and I am immensely happy. I open my heart and embrace everyone, with wine, music, and song. I offer my sincere words, forming a short chapter. The foundation has been laid, and progress is boundless. This is a model for the whole country, and the glory of Zhejiang."

Director Zhu Jiahua's Speech on Preparations 110

Reported that a Total of 185,500 Yuan in Donations were Received

Director Zhu Jiahua said in his speech: "Because I am busy with government affairs, I have had to rely on the help of the deputy directors. This place used to be the Sixth Division Garrison Headquarters. After it moved out a few months ago, we began to level the ground by two feet. The expenses were: 100,000 from Zhejiang, 10,000 from Jiangsu, 10,000 from Guangdong, 10,000 from Hubei, 10,000 from Hunan, 5,000 from Shandong, 3,000 from Anhui, 3,000 from Jiangxi, 3,000 from Shanghai, 3,000 from Hankou, 2,000 from Guizhou, 2,000 from Fujian, 1,500 from Qingdao, 1,000 from Liaoning, 1,000 from Henan, 500 from Heilongjiang, 500 from Jilin, and 20,000 from the central government, totaling 185,500 yuan."

Central Party Headquarters Shao Yuanchong's Address 111

Strengthen the National Physique

Complete the National Revolution

Shao Yuanchong, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, said in his address that for thousands of years, China has only focused on writing and has paid no attention to the national physique or the national spirit. Therefore, whenever foreign forces come to oppress us, we are often unable to resist. In recent years, Western white people have used their scientific spirit, and the Chinese nation has shown its weaknesses everywhere. Therefore, Sun Yat-sen advocated the National Revolution, not only to restore the inherent culture and morality, but also to restore the inherent abilities and national spirit, to strengthen the Chinese national physique, and to complete the National Revolution. This National Games has been prepared for a long time, and it can be held today. If the general public can recognize the mission of this conference, the country will have hope. Modern national citizens compete entirely on knowledge and ability, and it is essential to have a strong physique to revitalize culture, morality, and national spirit. Furthermore, sports should be widespread among all people, so that society as a whole can be strong, in order to become the best nation in the world, to create a new culture, and to develop national character. I hope that all athletes will recognize this important responsibility.

National Government Chairman Chiang's Address 112

The National Games is an Expression of Support for the Central Government

After the Speech, the Crowd Cheered "Long Live" Four Times

Chairman Chiang said briefly, "All members and chairmen of the National Games of the Republic of China, today we are holding the National Games here, and I will now report to you its meaning and mission. Our Chinese nation was the first to be civilized in the world, has a population of over 400 million, and occupies the first position in the world in terms of population. The land is also very vast. But what position does our country occupy in the world and in the international arena? Speaking of it is extremely shameful, but where does this great shame come from? It is caused by imperialists using various methods to oppress us. This National Games is an expression of the Chinese nation's demonstration against imperialism, an expression of an independent spirit, and also an expression against all warlords and reactionary forces within the country. This conference brings together the most outstanding and strongest citizens in the country in one place. In other words, it is an expression of unanimous support for the central government. Therefore, the meaning of this conference is not only to promote the national physique, but also to demonstrate against the imperialist warlords and reactionary forces in order to complete the National Revolution and build a country based on the Three Principles of the People, in order to wash away all past national humiliations. Today, on behalf of the National Government, I welcome athletes from all provinces and cities. From today onwards, I hope that you will continue to work hard in accordance with the mission of the conference." After Chairman Chiang finished his speech, he called out "Long Live the National Games," "Long Live the Chinese Nationalist Party," and "Long Live the Republic of China." The whole venue shouted, "Long Live Chairman Chiang."

Head Representative Yuan Lihun's Thank You Speech 113

Expressed Gratitude to the Conference

Hoped for Supervision from the Central Government

Head representative Yuan Lihun said in his address, "Today is the opening day of the unprecedented National Games in China. I, as the representative of the participating units, express my gratitude to the Chairman of the Central National Government and representatives from all parties. The opening of this National Games has been attended by representatives from the central government and various parties, giving us many lessons. In addition to encouraging ourselves to invigorate our spirits, we also thank the Central Government's address. Not only will we strive hard this time, but we will continue to promote sports after we leave. We, the participating units, have come to Hangzhou, and we are deeply honored by the thoroughness of the facilities and the warmth of the hospitality. I, as a representative, thank the organizing committee. This time the meeting is held in Hangzhou, which is a scenic spot in the country. In addition to participating in the meeting, we can also stroll around the mountains and rivers and recuperate our physical strength. I thank those who proposed the Hangzhou Games, and I thank the gentlemen who helped. Because the central government has promoted it so much, the facilities are so complete, and the location is so beautiful, we feel very gratified and inspired. We hope that after this meeting, sports will develop from now on, and the spirit will be universally healthy. I hope that the central government will supervise, and we will continue to work hard."

Chairman Chiang's Second Address 114

The Entire Meeting is the Best Way to Strengthen the Nation

After all the athletes from the provinces and cities took the oath, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the National Government delivered another address. He said briefly, "Athletes and comrades, I am afraid that my words just now were not very clear due to the strong wind. In order to express my full admiration, I would like to say a few more words to all athletes and comrades. Everyone is already very clear about the significance of holding this National Games, and the central government has even greater hopes for the National Games, because the foundation of the party and the country is the nation. If the nation is not strong, it will be invaded and encroached upon by foreign powers. The National Games is the best way to strengthen the nation. From this time on, the regions such as Kobe and Liaoning, which are far away, have been able to arrive on time to participate in the sports. This spirit is commendable. But in the face of the recent imperialist aggression and the oppression of warlord feudalism, I hope that everyone will use the spirit of participation to strengthen our bodies and rise up to fight," etc.

Wu Zhihui's Speech 115

We Must Be Civilized Citizens

Mr. Wu said briefly, "Today, it is not easy to gather athletes from all over the country in one place and hold such a grand sports meet. Originally, the strength or weakness of a country depends entirely on whether the national physique is strong or weak. Only with a strong nation can there be a strong country. The evolution of our population has a history of tens of thousands of years. Not only have we Chinese not evolved in terms of physique, but even our original physique has gradually degenerated, so that foreigners have given the name 'sick man of the East' to our citizens. I hope that all athletes will work hard from today onwards and be citizens of a civilized nation."

Wang Zhengting's Speech 116

The Conference is a Demonstration of the Spirit of National Unity

Hoped that the Delegation to the Far Eastern Games Would Achieve Final Victory

He generally said that the athletes had already heard many important speeches, so he didn't need to say much. However, he said that he was very happy to see so many athletes at this sports meeting. This sports meeting was initiated by Mr. Jingjiang [Zhang Jingjiang], and representatives from various provinces and overseas Chinese have come to participate. Therefore, Chairman Chiang said that the National Games can be regarded as a demonstration of the spirit of national unity. The Far Eastern Games will be held in Japan in May, so this conference can also be regarded as a preparatory meeting for the Far Eastern Games. I hope that the athletes who go to Japan will win glory for the motherland and achieve final victory, and promote the spirit of our nation.

Athletes from various provinces and cities stood in formation.

Photo by Xie Yuexi of Hangzhou

Chu Minyi's Speech 117

Hoped for a Grand Sports Meet Every Year

Mr. Chu said that he was very happy to participate in the National Games today. Because this National Games is the first conference after the unification of the National Government, he has participated in many provincial sports meets before and felt that the spirit and facilities were not as good as this time. This National Games was initiated by Mr. Jingjiang, with the purpose of stimulating the inherent physical education. However, physical education should be paid attention to at all times. On the one hand, there should be competitions, and on the other hand, more attention should be paid to regular practice. It is not a good phenomenon to pay attention only during competitions. I hope that there will be a grand sports meet every year in the future, so that physical education will be universal, and the physique of the people will change from weak to strong.

Soccer

Preliminary Round: Tianjin Overwhelming Victory Over Anhui 135

Nine to Zero

A total of eleven teams joined the soccer competition in this tournament. The competition adopted an elimination system. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the tournament opened at the soccer field. As a result, the Tianjin team overcame the Anhui team with a score of nine to zero. The lineups of the two teams and the match situation are recorded below.

Both Sides' Lineups 136

The Tianjin team launched fierce attacks on Anhui with its forwards. Both the left and right inside forwards were exceptionally lively. The Anhui team, on the other hand, was disorganized. Most of the balls kicked out were aimless, so they were always surrounded by the Tianjin team and had no chance of progress. As a result, the game was not exciting at all.

Tian Chen Fu Wang Fan Tian Zhu Zhang Sun Liang Bai Bai

Jin Er Xin Pei Shi Tian Zhi Chang Gui Jian Qing Yong

Team De Qiu Hua Kui Zhong Zhi Lian Yu Lin Wen Guo Xing

Position Goalkeeper Left Right Center Left Right Center Left Right Left Right

Internal Internal Forward Forward Internal Internal

Placement Guardian Guardian Hardened Guardian Guardian Forward Forward Forward Wing Wing

An Jiang Cao Zhang Zhang Cheng Wang Xu Zhou Zheng Bao Wang

Hui Jun Yuan Guang Zhi Jing Biyu Zhi Cheng Zi Zhao Dao

Team Xia Xun Zhao Yuan Li Biyu Bi Yu Kang Da Sheng

First Half: Four to Zero 137

After the start of the game, the Tianjin team forwards immediately launched a fierce attack on the Anhui goal. Tianjin team's Bai Anxing dribbled the ball and crossed it, but center forward Zhang Changyu's shot was blocked. However, surrounded on all sides, left inside forward Sun Guilin finally kicked it into the net. Anhui suffered a heavy blow from this and tried to recover, but their strength was ultimately insufficient, and they produced no results. Afterwards, Tianjin team's left winger Bai Qingguo dribbled the ball as if he were in no man's land and lifted his foot to shoot. The ball was obtained by Zhang Changyu, who passed it to Sun Guilin, who easily kicked it in again. After that, the Anhui team's formation became even more chaotic. Finally, Sun Guilin of the Tianjin team scored two goals in succession. The first half ended with a score of four to zero in favor of Tianjin.

Second Half: Five to Zero 138

After a five-minute break, the game continued. Not long after the start, Sun Guilin dribbled the ball straight in and scored another goal. This was only two minutes after the start of the half. At this time, the Anhui team's morale was even more shaken, and they missed every excellent opportunity. Afterwards, the ball was often in front of the Anhui team's goal, rarely crossing the halfway line. The Anhui team's goal became the target of everyone's attacks. Liang Jianwen also received assistance from the center forward and right winger and scored two goals. The eighth and ninth goals were both scored by center forward Zhang Changyu. Suddenly, the silver whistle sounded, and the game ended.

Men's Volleyball

Preliminary Round: Tianjin Complete Victory Over Zhejiang 139

Two to Zero

Once the sides were decided, Zhejiang served first. They did not score. Tianjin scored five consecutive points with their first serve, with great momentum. Then Zhejiang also tried to attack and made the score two to five. However, in the end, due to the huge difference in strength, it was difficult to resist. When the Tianjin team was ahead with a score of eleven to five, they switched sides. Their momentum became even stronger, and soon they won the first game with a score of twenty-one to five. In the second game, the Zhejiang team was still unable to recover and lost again with a score of four to twenty-one. The Tianjin team won two games in a row and won the right to the next match. The lineups of the two teams are listed below. The referee was Li Feiyun.

Men's Basketball

Preliminary Round: Tianjin Overwhelming Victory Over Jiangxi 142

First Sound: Tianjin Initially Shows Its Power

Strange Record: Jiangxi Almost Eats Dumplings

[A score of 153 to 4]

The tournament opened, and the basketball competition also began. Today's basketball program originally had three matches: Men's Shanxi vs. Anhui and Tianjin vs. Jiangxi, Women's Fujian vs. Shanghai. Later, since Shanxi and Fujian did not arrive, Shanghai and Anhui teams proceeded with a two-round competition. The Tianjin-Jiangxi battle started at 2:00 PM. This was the first act of the National Games basketball championship. Spectators flocked to the event, reaching over a thousand people. Referee Qian Yiqin and Inspector Shao Ji arrived at the venue and ordered the game to begin. Tianjin immediately took the offensive. In less than a minute, center Liu Jianchang scored a basket, opening the scoring. Not long after, Jiangxi had a free throw opportunity, and Hu Xianmei made one point, making the score two to one. Tianjin had many Nankai team members, and their exquisite skills were well known to people across the country. Most of Jiangxi's players were emerging athletes, and their skills were naturally slightly inferior. Tianjin forwards Tang Baokun, Yao Enhan, and Liu Jianchang passed the ball to each other, scoring repeatedly. Jiangxi was unable to fight back. Tianjin then replaced reserve players to continue the battle, but their momentum did not weaken at all. As a result of the first half, Tianjin scored 63 points, while Jiangxi only scored one point. After a ten-minute break, they switched sides and continued the battle. Tianjin's momentum was still strong. Jiangxi suffered a complete defeat. The final score was one hundred fifty-three to four, a difference of one hundred forty-nine points, a strange record unprecedented in the basketball world. Looking at the overall game, both teams gave their all in the battle. One side did not become arrogant because of their victory, and the other side did not become discouraged because of their defeat. Both sides fought to the end, and their perseverance and spirit were commendable.

Congratulatory Telegrams from Various Leaders 148

Wang Chonghui: To the National Games, Mr. Zhang Jingjiang, Dai Jitao, He Jingzhi, Zhu Liuxian, and other gentlemen. Upon receiving the invitation to go to Hangzhou to observe the National Games, I very much wanted to go. Unfortunately, today I am going to Zhenjiang to supervise an oath-taking ceremony and cannot participate in the grand event. I am very sorry. I respectfully wish the sports meet great success in promoting and guiding the nation. Your brother, Wang Chonghui.

Chen Hexian: To National Games Chairman Dai, Vice-Chairman He: I was officially recommended by the Jiangsu Provincial Government to participate in the grand opening of the Games tomorrow. However, it coincides with the oath-taking ceremony for the new Jiangsu Provincial Committee and the heads of various departments, and I am unable to arrive in Hangzhou on time. I plan to go for sightseeing a day or two later. I hereby send this telegram for your understanding. Chen Hexian bows.

People Attending the Games 149

The National Games officially opened in Hangzhou yesterday. Shanghai, as one of the most important regions in the country, not only sent athletes to participate but also organized a delegation to attend the opening ceremony and assist the organizing committee in handling all matters. To show the importance of the delegation, the municipal government specifically appointed Chen Dezheng, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, as the Chief Representative. Mr. Chen went to Hangzhou the day before yesterday to attend as a representative. All business related to the Education Bureau will be handled on his behalf by Section Chief Ni Wenya.

The National Games is scheduled to be held in Hangzhou on April 1st. The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously resolved to officially recommend Director Chen of the Education Department to go to Hangzhou to attend the ceremony. Mr. Chen originally planned to go early, but the new Jiangsu Provincial Committee and the heads of various departments are scheduled to take office and swear oaths on that day, making it impossible to leave. Therefore, Mr. Chen has changed his plan to go for sightseeing after the inauguration and has already telegraphed Chairman Dai and Vice-Chairmen Zhang and He of the Sports Federation to discuss the matter.

Yang Zhongming, the chief representative of Anhui Province, was originally the Director of the General Affairs Department of the Preparatory Office of the Central China Games. Due to the closing of the Preparatory Office, he was unable to accompany the athletes of the province. Mr. Yang took an express overnight trip to the East because of the opening of the Games and arrived late at night on the 31st.

Ling Daoyang, Captain of the Capital Tennis Team 150

Athlete Life 151

Clothing: Athletes from all directions gather at this National Games, truly making it a grand occasion. The clothes usually worn by the athletes are colorful and very impressive. In addition to most wearing ordinary sports clothes, the female athletes from Liaoning wear violet sports caps and purple-red velvet shirts with blue trim, with dark blue serge trousers and shirts. The female athletes from Beiping wear black velvet shirts with red trim and black shirts and trousers. The female athletes from Qingdao wear blue cloth shirts and blue cloth skirts. The male athletes wear yellow velvet shirts and white trousers, and the male athletes from Hebei wear red velvet shirts and white trousers. The colors are all well-coordinated and very beautiful. In general, the colors of clothes in North China are very bright, while the clothes of athletes in Central China, such as Hunan, Henan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, are very simple. This alone is enough to show the psychology of clothing colors in the country.

Food: There are more than 3,000 athletes and staff members at the Games, making the issue of food very important. The organizing committee has contracted with the Bao Shi Kitchen Army for meals and has set a treaty to have lunch at 12:00 PM and dinner at 6:00 PM every day, simultaneously, without delay, to facilitate time. It is also stipulated that there are eight athletes per table, with four dishes, two bowls, and one soup, costing 20 cents per person. Staff members have six bowls and one soup, with six people per table, costing 20 cents per person. However, if the organizing committee opens meals at the same time, there is no such wide hall in the venue to accommodate the need for a big meal. Therefore, a large shed has been built, measuring eleven rooms wide and twenty rooms deep, with 240 tables and 960 benches, allowing for simultaneous meals. The sound of plates and bowls echoes. The four words "spectacular sight" are enough to describe such a large dining hall. On the first day of the meal, the northern athletes raised objections, because northerners prefer noodles and find it difficult to swallow white rice. The organizing committee also took into account the different habits between the North and the South, so the white rice for the northern athletes was changed to bread and large steamed buns for each meal.

Many slogans related to eating are posted in the large dining hall. They are recorded as follows: "Eating is 'group-oriented'," "Eat to your heart's content," "Buckle up and exercise," "Win the championship with a full stomach," "Neatness at meals can be seen in the neatness of exercise," "Chew while eating, do not speak." The use of slogans for eating is truly a first for the National Games.

All Instructors

Accommodation: The Games venue is located in Meidong Gaoqiao, originally an old barracks, covering an area of 300 acres. The venue is all open space, while the offices in the rear are in the barracks. Therefore, the athletes' dormitories are transformations of the barracks. There are three dormitories: the first is for women, and the second and third are for men. Each room in the first has 32 beds, with wooden frames in two layers, like upper and lower bunks on a ship, for a total of more than 2,000 beds. Each dormitory has two laborers to take care of everything. The women's dormitories are even more well-equipped. Each room has a piece of white cloth at the door as a screen, and there are 20 bathtubs, specifically for the female athletes to cleanse themselves. Nine female servants have been hired, one in charge of the pavilion, four as errand girls, and four to manage the bathroom. Two female receptionists have also been hired to handle reception matters. As for laundry and various other trivial matters, all equipment can be described as meticulous. However, some athletes, such as the athletes from Guangdong, feel that the beds in the dormitory are made of hardwood and are unwilling to endure it, so they all reside in the West Lake Hotel.

Odds and Ends

Among the Hydrangea Bushes 152

When the Games were about to open, the female athletes from all over could not help but have their hearts beating. Although they usually trained well, they were still worried about not being accurate, and even more so because of their vanity and competitive spirit, they practiced desperately. Some had lovers guiding them by their side, practicing volleyball in the square, their voices娇声引吭. Red and green clusters formed round shapes, like several hydrangea flowers laid flat. The spectators also almost felt as if they were in a flower bush.

Female Students in the Stands

Photo by Xie Yuexi, Hangzhou

Confusing and Bewildering 153

Before the opening, boys and girls from elementary schools in Hangzhou gathered in the inner square of the preparatory office, with glowing spirits and innocent expressions. The boys and girls wore white caps, white cloth jackets, and blue bamboo cloth trousers. The girls wore blue bamboo cloth skirts. The colors were distinct, but at a glance, the upper bodies were all white and the lower bodies were all blue, making it difficult to distinguish male from female.

On the Independent High Platform 154

Honorary Chairman Chiang Kai-shek arrived at the meeting that day with his wife, Soong Mei-ling, with joy overflowing between their eyebrows. When the master of ceremonies announced the Chairman's speech, Chiang saw a photography stage in the middle of the venue, so he ordered to leave his seat and ascend the stage to give his speech. As the photography stage was not located in the center of the venue, the police and the audience moved it to the center. Chiang gracefully ascended, wearing a light yellow military uniform, looking high and far, reaching out in all directions, speaking and pointing, with a strong voice and spirit, which encouraged the athletes greatly.

Earnest Words 155

A broadcasting wireless machine was installed in front of the rostrum. When Chiang moved to the venue to give his speech, the machine was quickly moved and installed. By the time it was installed, Chiang had already finished speaking. After returning to the rostrum, after speeches by guests such as Wu Zhihui, Wang Zhengting, and Chu Minyi, Chiang was afraid that everyone had not fully understood his first speech, so he repeated it on the broadcasting machine, with thunderous applause.

Prizes Piled into a Tower 156

The opening ceremony of the Games was held at the athletics field. In the middle of the field, a long pole was erected to hang flags. When the reporter entered the field at about 7:00, the Games staff were stacking prizes into a tower around the pole. There were no fewer than two or three hundred silver goblets and shields. It was said that this was only a quarter of the prizes.

Boating on the Lake and Gouging Cucumbers 157

Athletes from various provinces had arrived in Hangzhou ten days before the Games. Now that the Six Bridges and Three Temples were full of peach blossoms and green willows, the athletes went for a boat ride on the lake in their free time. Therefore, traces of athletes could be seen everywhere on the embankment and in the lake. However, the Games venue and its surroundings were not located in the city center, and people rarely visited there on weekdays. Now that so many athletes had suddenly come, the rickshaw pullers who stayed there took the opportunity to exploit them. The boatmen by the lake usually raised their prices for tourists, and now that it was springtime and the athletes had accents from other places, the boatmen ganged up to gouge them, so the daily rate for boat rides, which was usually one yuan, cost no less than two or three yuan these days.

Not Shedding the Northern Air 158

The rest rooms for male and female athletes were clearly marked in the venue. Yesterday, after the athletics competition, three female athletes from Liaoning, feeling tired, lay down on the floor of the Liaoning male athletes' rest room. The male athletes next to them were either lying down or sitting on the floor. According to the traditions of the North, men and women, or guests, often lie together to keep warm and do not find it strange. Spectators passing by often stopped to watch.

Many Interesting Things at Night 159

Last night, a female athlete from Shanghai, feeling idle, saw a rickshaw in front of the dormitory and impersonated a rickshaw puller, pulling it to the southeast corner of the field near the gate. A male athlete happened to be going out and shouted from afar, "Hey, rickshaw!" The female athlete deliberately made a funny gesture, speaking in her Shanghai accent, "Where to? Come, come!" When they got closer and looked at each other, they burst out laughing.

Chairman Chiang and His Wife

Photo by Xie Yuexi, Hangzhou

Trying to Be Clever and Making a Mess 160

At the opening ceremony, there was initially a slight breeze, which then turned into a strong wind. When Chiang gave his second speech, the Zhejiang Provincial Party Department took advantage of the wind to scatter leaflets, blowing them to the crowd like snowflakes, dancing wildly in the air. The leaflets urged the use of domestic goods, but the rostrum was also obscured by the flying catkins, making it difficult to see clearly. The police department immediately prohibited this and threatened to punish them for disrupting order, which was truly trying to be clever and making a mess.

A Sense of Incompleteness 161

The female athletes from various places all had short hair and short clothes, with their chests sticking out, giving the impression of strong warriors. However, Yin Linzhen, number 252 in volleyball, a female athlete from Shanghai, was short and petite, and still had a braid behind her, which had not been cut off, inevitably giving people a sense of incompleteness.

Added Items for the Central China Games 165

Starting from the next session, women's indoor baseball will be added

Among the sports items of the Central China Games, women only have basketball, team ball, and tennis. There is no soccer or baseball for women. At this meeting held in Anhui, the representatives of each province discussed and decided to add women's indoor baseball starting from the next session. This means that there will be one more item for women's sports in the next Central China Games.

All-Day Preliminary Meeting

(1) Meeting of the Japan Sports Association 166

According to a Tokyo correspondent from this newspaper on March 27, the Japan Sports Association held a general affairs committee meeting at the Tokyo Central Pavilion at 6:00 PM on the 26th of this month. The attendees included President Kiyokazu Kishi, Vice President Hiranuma, and more than 20 committee members. The following matters were resolved:

1. It was decided to add mechanical gymnastics to this session of the Games.

2. The winning country of each competition and event will be allowed to simultaneously hoist its national flag and the flag of its affiliated organization.

3. The call for the Games theme song previously offered a reward and received a total of 350 entries. Reviewers Takanura and Dozaki have been commissioned to review them.

4. A total of 250 types of slogans for the Games were received, and the results will be announced on the 31st.

(II) Japan National Track and Field Meet 167

Tokyo Correspondence, March 27th. Japan, in order to select track and field representatives to participate in the Far Eastern Games, held the National Track and Field Meet at the Meiji Jingu Stadium in Tokyo on the 26th of this month. As a result, several astonishing new Far Eastern records were produced. The names, scores, and school affiliations of the athletes are recorded below:

(III) Japan Strenuously Practices Soccer 168

The soccer representatives for Japan for the third Far Eastern Games have already been selected. The main players are from the two teams of Tokyo University and Kwansei Gakuin University. Mr. Takekoshi is the coach and commander. Every day he leads vigorous practice sessions at the Jingu Stadium. Because Japanese soccer has historically been immature, in order to arouse the enthusiasm and effort of the players, a soccer players' motivational meeting was held at the Asahi Hall a few days ago. Sports expert Mr. Imamura delivered an earnest speech, hoping that Japanese players could keep pace with China. In order to promote soccer tactics, Japan will provide substantial rewards and preferential treatment to soccer players.

Chairman Chiang on the Rostrum

The Renaming and Methods for Chinese Medicine Schools 169

The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Health have submitted a request to the government and the Executive Yuan to change the names of Chinese medicine schools to Chinese Medicine Academies and to manage them according to the methods for managing academic groups, in accordance with the law. An order has recently been issued to the Education Bureaus of various provinces and special municipalities. The case involves Proclamation No. 8 issued by this Ministry last year, which changed Chinese medicine schools into training centers, and the Ministry of Health's order changing Chinese medicine hospitals into clinics, prohibiting Chinese medicine practitioners from using Western instruments and medicines. These cases have been submitted to the Executive Yuan, which has been informed by a letter from the Civil Affairs Office of the National Government that it has received an instruction from Chairman Chiang to revoke the aforementioned proclamations and orders, and to comply with the instructions. Upon receiving this instruction, we should respectfully adhere to Chairman Chiang's intention to protect Chinese medicine and comply with the instructions. Subsequently, in February of this year, this Ministry, together with the Ministry of Health, submitted a report to the Executive Yuan, detailing the circumstances of changing the names of Chinese medicine schools, allowing Chinese medicine practitioners to use Western instruments, and changing Chinese medicine hospitals into medical clinics. This Ministry proposed changing Chinese medicine schools into Chinese Medicine Academies, and the Ministry of Health proposed changing the names of hospitals, with better public Chinese medicine hospitals being called "Public Chinese Medicine Hospital of..." We requested that these proposals be forwarded to the National Government for review and compliance. Subsequently, the Chairman of the Executive Yuan, Zhu Jiahua, delivered an opening speech at the meeting.

Photograph by Xie Yuexi, Hangzhou

The Executive Yuan has ordered that the proposed methods be implemented separately, adhering to the law while also embodying the intention to protect Chinese medicine. This has been forwarded for approval to facilitate implementation. Furthermore, we have received an order stating that the National Government has approved the instruction and ordered its implementation, in addition to separate orders to the Ministry of Health. Upon receiving these instructions, we should comply. Regarding the method proposed by this Ministry to change Chinese medicine schools into Chinese Medicine Academies, it is for the sake of improving Chinese medicine. We should conduct scientific research and improvements on existing academic knowledge and clinical experience, so that it gradually becomes a scientific discipline. Students studying Chinese medicine should first have this foundation before pursuing further studies. During this transitional period, Chinese medicine should move towards science and free research. Therefore, we specifically request that the organization of the place for researching Chinese medicine be called Chinese Medicine Academy, so that it can become an academic group and be managed according to the methods for educational administrative agencies managing academic groups. Hereafter, all Chinese medicine schools within the jurisdiction of the "Office" or "Bureau" should be instructed to change their names to Chinese Medicine Academies. All management methods should be implemented in accordance with the methods for educational administrative agencies managing academic groups. In addition to separate orders, we are hereby issuing an order for compliance.

Labour University Touring Group Sets Off in Different Directions 170

The National Labour University in Jiangwan has organized a spring vacation touring group to investigate labour education and social conditions in various regions, hoping to mutually verify what they have learned. It is planned to organize two routes: Hangzhou and Wuxi. The Hangzhou team consists of approximately 200 students from the three colleges of Engineering, Society, and Agriculture, as well as the affiliated high school. The Wuxi team consists of approximately 30 students. Yesterday morning, they set off by train in different directions. Each person carried various survey forms, and the department heads and staff members were responsible for guidance. In the future, the results of the tour will undoubtedly contribute greatly to society.

Local News

The Two Courts of the Public Concession Established Yesterday 171

The Presidents and Prosecutors of Both Courts Take Office

Each Gives a Speech on Justice and Integrity

Representatives of the Party Hope to Eradicate Bad Habits

Yesterday Afternoon, Cases Accumulated by the Police Stations Were Heard

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and the Shanghai Special District Court were officially established yesterday at the original site of the provisional court on North Zhejiang Road. The presidents of both courts and the chief prosecutors of both courts, as well as all the prison directors, were sworn into office at the same time. Ma Shouhua, a director specially appointed by the Ministry of Judicial Administration, came to Shanghai to supervise the oath-taking ceremony. The detailed situation is recorded as follows:

Court Arrangement: At the main entrance of the court facing North Zhejiang Road, the flags of the Party and the country are crossed. Above, a long wooden plaque reading "Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court" is hung, and below, a long wooden plaque reading "Shanghai Special District Court of Jiangsu" is hung. Both are in black characters on a white background. Above the main entrance hangs a white cloth banner reading "The World is for All". On both sides are white cloths written with the couplet "The Revolution Has Not Yet Succeeded" and "Comrades Still Need to Strive". The entrance to the main entrance is the registration office, with a signature book and several receptionists to receive guests. After signing in, the receptionists lead the guests to the reception room or auditorium on the second floor of the High Court branch.

A Glimpse of the Auditorium: The auditorium for the oath-taking ceremony is located in the second courtroom on the second floor of the High Court branch. In the center of the auditorium, a portrait of Sun Yat-sen and his will are hung, with the flags of the Party and the country crossed above, and the two characters "Auditorium" written on white cloth. There is also a banner with "The World is for All", and the couplet "The Revolution Has Not Yet Succeeded" and "Comrades Still Need to Strive". Oath Order

Photography of the Inauguration Ceremony of Presidents Xu and Yang (Taken by China Photo Studio)

Notable Guests: Among the guests, Pan Gongzhan was present from the Municipal Party Department, Su Fuchou from the Garrison Headquarters, Yu Hongjun from the Municipal Government, Guan Jiongzhi from the Stamp Duty Bureau, and Yu Qiaqing and Chen Bingqian from the business community. The largest number of guests were from the legal profession, including famous lawyers Chen Tingrui, Jiang Yiping, Wu Chengyu, Shen Yuesheng, Qin Liankui, Fan Gang, Qu Yue, and others. Female guests included Dr. Zheng Yuxiu and Mrs. Xu, and the daughter of Court President Hu. The hall was crowded with three or four hundred people.

Inauguration Ceremony: The inauguration was originally scheduled for 10 a.m., but due to various procedural delays, it was not until 11 a.m. that Presidents Xu and Yang, Chief Prosecutors Wang and Zhou, Prison Director Xie, and the presidents, judges, and prosecutors of the civil and criminal divisions of the two courts successively entered the auditorium. The master of ceremonies, Xiong Sipeng, called out according to the pre-arranged order: (1) The supervising officer takes the chair, (2) The president of the High Court branch, the chief prosecutor of the High Court branch, the president of the Special District Court, the chief prosecutor of the Special District Court, and the second prison director take their places, (3) The entire hall stands at attention, (4) The chairman respectfully reads the will, (5) Three minutes of silence, (6) The chairman presents the seals, (7) Oath-taking (the oath is recorded below), (8) Admonitory speech by the supervising officer, (9) Speech by the representative of the Party, (10) Speech by the guest, (11) Responses from the president and chief prosecutor (all speeches are recorded below).

Text of the Oath: I solemnly swear that I will恪恪恪遵 Sun Yat-sen's will, obey the Party's principles, abide by the laws of the nation, be loyal and diligent in my duties, and save expenses. I resolve not to hire useless personnel, not to engage in private gain or corruption, and not to accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment from the Party. I swear. First, President Xu raised his right hand and respectfully read the above oath, and ordered all the prosecutors of both courts to follow him, each raising their right hand. Then, Chief Prosecutor Wang of the High Court, President Yang of the District Court, Chief Prosecutor Zhou, and Prison Director Xie each raised their right hand in turn and read the oath aloud.

Admonitory Speech by the Supervising Officer: Ma Shouhua, Director of the Ministry of Judicial Administration and supervising officer, gave an admonitory speech, stating in brief: Today is the day of the establishment of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and the Shanghai Special District Court, and it is also the day of the oath-taking ceremony for the presidents and chief prosecutors of both courts. I have been ordered by the Ministry of Judicial Administration to come here to supervise the oath-taking, and I would like to offer a few words and express my expectations. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it has now entered the period of political tutelage, and construction is of utmost importance. The judicial authorities are working hard to protect human rights, and the establishment of the two courts is timely. Although their organization and powers are still limited by special circumstances, they are generally similar to purely Chinese courts. The unequal treatment that the people of the Special District have suffered in the past can be gradually eliminated, and the presidents and all the judges of the two courts are always honest and just, and can all do their best to abide by the law. I believe that they will surely live up to the wishes of the people of the Special District. However, at the beginning of this reform, I hope that they will work even harder to ensure that the property, reputation, and freedom of all the people in the Special District are fully protected by law. As for honesty and justice, these are well-known and easily practiced by all the presidents and prosecutors, and I need not elaborate further.

Speech by the Party Department: Pan Gongzhan, representative of the Special Municipal Party Department, gave a speech, stating in brief: Today, I am very honored to participate in this grand ceremony. I represent the Municipal Party Department and should offer a few words. I recall that a few months ago, I came here to attend the inauguration ceremony of President Xu as the president of the Provisional Court. At that time, I earnestly hoped that President Xu would overthrow all the distorted systems of the past decades, especially the last twenty years, and establish a court that fully conformed to the general legal system. Fortunately, the efforts of the various departments of the Central Government have made this hope a reality. Although there are still one or two points that cannot satisfy people's wishes due to environmental factors, they must be reformed gradually and cannot be achieved overnight. Now, the prison has been taken back and the three-trial system has been implemented. Other distortions will eventually be eliminated, and it is expected that those that cannot be satisfied can also be gradually improved. I hope that all the judges will work hard and be able to achieve their goals. We also believe that all the judges led by the presidents of the two courts will be able to fulfill their duties. Sun Yat-sen said that knowing is difficult, but doing is easy. Justice and integrity are well-known to judges, but sometimes they are not honest. This is because their will is weak, and they fall when they are tempted. Therefore, those who know must know thoroughly, so that they will not be swayed by the environment, and the people can receive just benefits. Shanghai is the easiest place to violate the law and lose one's personality and morals. I believe that the presidents of the two courts will be able to establish a good reputation and set an example here. Therefore, I have sincere hope for the presidents of the two courts and all the prosecutors to proceed with justice and integrity. There is also one point: the prosecutors and prison directors have always been honest and self-disciplined, but they cannot rely solely on the honesty of their superiors. All the staff must have a sense of justice and integrity in order to be effective. If you want your subordinates to be honest, you must strictly assess them. Otherwise, if only the superiors are honest, it will not alleviate the suffering of the people in litigation. Furthermore, if subordinates are deceived or obstructed in their work, and those who suffer have no way to complain, they can only swallow their anger and weep silently. Superiors will still not know the pain of the people. I am not usually good at flattery, but today I have the opportunity to congratulate the wise leaders on their inauguration, so I am fulfilling my responsibility to speak my mind. I hope that all the bad habits of the past can be completely eradicated. I have heard that there is a lot of corruption in prisons and detention centers. Prisons are still tolerable, but detention centers hold people who have not been convicted, and they also suffer, and they suffer without daring to complain, and without a way to complain. They only tell their relatives and friends after they are released, and never complain in public. I hope that after this reform, the wise leaders will pay attention to these small details, because those who can truly connect with the people are mostly subordinates. If you want to alleviate their suffering, you should strictly assess your subordinates, and strive to eliminate one thing at a time, and work hard one day at a time to achieve results. What I have contributed today is entirely on behalf of those who have suffered in prisons and detention centers, appealing to the wise leaders.

Speech by the Guest: Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, representing the Mayor of the Special Municipality, Zhang Qun, gave a speech, stating in general: The establishment of the High Court branch and the Special District Court gradually completes the judicial system in the Special District. From now on, I deeply hope that the court and the municipal government will fully cooperate so that the people can benefit, and I hope that it will become a model court for the whole country.

Summary of Responses: (1) President Xu of the High Court branch said in his speech: Today is the first day that the Shanghai Special District has formed a formal court. The officials of the two courts and the branch prison are taking office at the same time. The Party Department and the responsible department have given us earnest instructions. We should strictly abide by them. I personally have no opinion to express, but whether the officials of the two courts and the branch prison are qualified is not only related to local security and the rights of the people, but also has an impact on current and future diplomacy. I hope that my colleagues will abide by the law in everything they do, and that all sectors of society will uphold the law, so that the credibility of the court can be maintained, and the foreign policy that Sun Yat-sen has proclaimed will eventually be completely victorious. This is what I use to encourage myself, and I would like to share it with everyone present. (2) Chief Prosecutor Wang Zhennan of the High Court branch said in his response: I will sincerely accept the admonitory speech of the supervising officer of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, the guidance of the representative of the Municipal Party Department, and the expectations of the guests regarding integrity. As for the current prosecutorial system and prosecutorial powers, I feel that there are still limitations in the agreement. In addition, I should strive to fully exercise my powers and work hard. (3) President Yang Zhaoyu of the Special District Court said in his response: The instructions of the representative of the Ministry of Justice, the guidance of the representative of the Party Department, and the opinions expressed by the guests should be regarded as golden rules, and it is especially important to abide by the law. I will encourage all the judges to do so. (4) Chief Prosecutor Zhou Xianjue of the Special District Court said in his response: The prosecutorial system in the Special District has just been established, and foreigners are initially unclear about it, causing many obstacles and preventing prosecutors from fully exercising their powers. We should work hard to eliminate foreigners' doubts, and integrity is what I have always upheld, and I should practice it in my own life.

Photography and Adjournment: The meeting adjourned at noon. The group went downstairs and sat in a semi-circle outside the main entrance of the court to take pictures. After the event, the guests dispersed, and Presidents Xu and Yang sat down again with the presidents, judges, and prosecutors of the two courts in turn, still in a semi-circle, to take another picture as a memento. When taking office in the auditorium, electric light photos were also taken three times. Everyone in the auditorium was startled by the loud noise.

Inauguration Announcements: (1) Announcement No. 1 of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, for the purpose of announcement. It is hereby announced that Xu Weizhen has been appointed as the President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, and Wang Zhennan has been appointed as the Chief Prosecutor of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, etc., in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Judicial Administration. The President and Chief Prosecutor of this court have taken the oath of office today, in accordance with the order. This announcement is hereby issued for public information. April 19, 19 of the Republic of China, President Xu Weizhen, Chief Prosecutor Wang Zhennan. (2) Announcement No. 1 of the Shanghai Special District Court of Jiangsu, for the purpose of announcement. It is hereby announced that Yang Zhaoyu has been appointed as the President of the Shanghai Special District Court, and has been ordered to take the oath of office on April 1, in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and the order of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The President of this court has taken the oath of office on April 1, in accordance with the order. This announcement is hereby issued for public information. (3) Announcement No. 1 of the Chief Prosecutor of the Shanghai Special District Court, for the purpose of announcement. It is hereby announced that Zhou Xianjue has been appointed as the Chief Prosecutor of the Shanghai Special District Court of Jiangsu, in accordance with Order No. 594 of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and has been ordered to take the oath of office on April 1, in accordance with the order of the Chief Prosecutor of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The Chief Prosecutor of this court has taken the oath of office today, in accordance with the order. This announcement is hereby issued for public information. (4) Announcement by the Director of the Prison, for the purpose of announcement. It is hereby announced that Xie Fuzi has been temporarily appointed as the Director of the Second Branch Prison of Jiangsu, and the Director of the Detention Center of the Shanghai Special District Court, and the Director of the Civil Detention Center, etc., in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Judicial Administration of the National Government's Judicial Yuan. The Director of this prison has assumed office on the first day of this month, and this order is hereby issued for general knowledge.

Change of Names: The offices and courtrooms of the two courts were all assigned yesterday. All the old buildings, except for Courtroom 14, belong to the High Court branch, and the newly built buildings, including Courtroom 14 of the old buildings, are assigned to the Special District Court. The High Court branch has three courtrooms, namely Courtrooms 1, 2, and 3. The District Court has ten courtrooms, namely Courtrooms 5 to 14. The names of the courts are now marked on the doors of each courtroom and office to distinguish them. However, the bail room is still located in the building assigned to the High Court branch and has not been moved. The male detention center for civil cases has been changed to the Civil Detention Center of the Shanghai Special District Court. Two wooden plaques with the names of the Second Branch Prison of Jiangsu and the Detention Center of the Shanghai Special District Court are hung on both sides of the entrance to the female detention center to correct the names.

Afternoon Hearings: All cases that had been suspended since the Yellow Flower Mound Memorial Day, followed by the weekend and the handover, had not been heard for four days until yesterday. President Yang, fearing a backlog of cases, instructed all the police stations to send all the new cases and pending cases handled in recent days to the court for hearing at 2 p.m. yesterday. A total of 139 new and old cases of all sizes were sent to the court by the various police stations, and were heard by the four courtrooms, namely the first, second, fifth, and seventh courtrooms. The prosecutors also attended court with the judges to perform their duties. This was the first hearing after the establishment of the Special District Court. The hearing procedure and formalities were roughly the same as in the Provisional Court era, except that there was no consular observer, and a prosecutor was added to express his opinion after the end of the debate.

Chairman Chiang Arrives in Shanghai from Hangzhou This Morning 172

Residing at the New Longhua Railway Station

Will Take the Original Special Train to Nanjing

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and his wife of the National Government went to Ningbo and then to Hangzhou. Yesterday morning, they participated in the opening ceremony of the National Games, and then at 8:30 p.m. last night, accompanied by Finance Minister Song Ziwen, Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, German military advisor Fischer, and guards, they left Hangzhou for Shanghai by special train. The armored car Nanjing No. 1 led the way. They arrived at New Longhua Station at 0:30 this morning. Chairman Chiang and his wife and party stayed in the car and spent the night at the station. At 6:30 this morning, they left New Longhua Station and headed for the North Station. It is expected that after arriving at the North Station, they will take the original special train directly to Nanjing. However, their family members prepared a car this morning and waited for Chiang at the North Station. Upon learning of Chiang's arrival in Shanghai, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters deployed soldiers from the Fifth Division and spread out sentries in New Longhua, Xujiahui, Fanwangdu, and the North Station to provide all-night protection.

The Social Affairs Bureau Warns Rice Merchants Against Speculation 173

The rice market was still very tense yesterday. Only eight rice boats arrived at the south city riverbank, and only one of them came from Tongli. According to the investigation, there were fourteen boats of rice from Tongli arriving in port on the 28th of last month. In this situation, it is obvious that someone is manipulating the market. In addition, boatman Zhang Liandi had 120 piculs of Lian Tang Bo rice on board, which arrived in port on the 27th of last month and was docked at the new pier. As of yesterday, more than 90 piculs had not been sold, hoping for a good price. At a time of food panic, it is truly a scourge of the people's livelihood to engage in hoarding and price gouging. After receiving the report, the Social Affairs Bureau immediately convened the boatman and the dealer, Wanxing Rice Shop, to the bureau together with the Public Security Bureau to give them a warning. In the future, when rice boats arrive in port, they should be sold immediately without waiting or hoarding. It was also found that there were cases of waiting and not selling in the northern part of the city. The bureau also investigated and issued strict warnings at the time.

And Established a Party Branch at the Same Time

The new Minquan warship of the Navy held a flag-raising ceremony at 8 a.m. yesterday. Male and female guests arrived one after another, about a hundred people. The order of the ceremony was as follows: (1) Stand at attention and sing the Party song, (2) Bow three times to the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (3) The captain respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will, (4) Raise the flag, (5) Award the seal, (6) Commander Chen's speech, (7) Captain Luo sworn in, (8) Free speech, (9) End of ceremony, photography. Commander Chen inspected the enemy defense exercise. In an instant, the bugles sounded in unison, and the entire ship was ready for battle. The guns were operated freely, and the transmission of ammunition and fire fighting were all in accordance with orders. There was silence, and the guests were moved and held their breath to watch. After the exercise, Commander Chen gave another encouraging speech, and the tea party ended. In the afternoon, a party branch was established. The following is a quick record of the speech. Since the establishment of the National Government, in the past two years, our Navy has successively built the Xianning and Yongxu warships. It can be imagined that the leaders of the country attach importance to naval construction and that Vice Minister Chen Shaokuan has put a lot of effort into planning. Now, the Minquan, which was subsequently built by the Jiangnan Shipyard, has also been completed. Today, the flag-raising ceremony is held, and Captain Luo is taking office on the same day. Xunyong is very happy to be ordered by the Navy Department to come to the ship to supervise the oath. I hope that the construction of our country's warships will become more prosperous day by day in order to strengthen our national defense. I especially hope that all colleagues will work together with one heart and one mind for the preservation of the new

Page 14

ship and the work of training, and strive to fulfill our duties to strengthen our military might. I wish the National Government longevity, the revolutionary Navy longevity, and the officers and men of the Navy and the Minquan warship longevity. The ship was originally scheduled to sail to Ningbo yesterday, but because the wireless radio was not yet installed, it was changed to export today.

The Municipal Land Bureau Sets a Deadline for Converting Foreign Merchants' Dao Deeds 177

From April 1st to July 31st

After the Deadline, a Certificate from the Relevant Consul General Is Required

The Municipal Land Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: For the purpose of announcement, after this bureau took over the Foreign Merchants' Land Survey Bureau of the former Shangbao Association, since 1919 of the Republic of China, all foreign nationals who lease land from Chinese people shall obtain a permanent lease issued by this bureau. The Dao deed shall be converted within two months from the date of signing the contract; otherwise, it will be invalid. All old lease contracts established before 1919 of the Republic of China that have not yet been converted to Dao deeds shall be requested for conversion to Dao deeds within four months from April 1st to July 31st, 1919. It will be invalid after the deadline. Those who cannot convert to Dao deeds within four months must have sufficient reasons and present a letter of proof from the relevant Consul General before the conversion will be approved. In addition to sending a letter to the Consuls General of various countries stationed in Shanghai for reference, this announcement is hereby issued for general knowledge to foreign nationals of all countries.

Director Wu Discusses Dredging Yu Tang 178

The Yu Tang River in the western countryside of Shanghai County has recently become increasingly silted. The County Construction Bureau's Second, Third, and Sixth Districts, along with local gentry, have initiated preparations for dredging. Wu Wenhua, Director of the Construction Bureau, is scheduled to meet with representatives from the districts and local figures today to conduct a renewed survey as a basis for action. Yesterday, Director Wu spoke in detail about the history of Yu Tang and the dredging plan, which is closely related to water conservancy. A record of this follows:

Yu Tang is the main east-west river in the county, receiving water from the Xiepu River in the east and reaching the Songjiang boundary in the west to connect with Lake Mao. It stretches over 4,700 zhang, equivalent to more than 27 li. The tributary rivers it receives include Yu'erjing, Zhangshugang, Lijia Gang, Daijia Gang, Dian Gang, Sha Gang, Zi Gang, Zhu Gang, Miao Jing, Heng Jing, Xin Gou, Xing Dou He, and Tangcun Jing. These rivers irrigate a total of over 54,000 mu of farmland. The eastern region is suitable for cotton, while the western countryside is suitable for rice. All water resources are drawn from here. Because the Huangpu River receives sea tides in the east, with muddy water entering and clear water leaving, silt accumulates easily. Therefore, the county records indicate that there was originally a rule of dredging every five years after periods of flooding or drought. However, since the dredging in the nineteenth year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, over 30 years have passed, and the siltation has become increasingly severe. Boats and ships can barely pass. Repeated military disasters, a lack of attention, and the impoverished state of the people have made it difficult to start construction. The matter has been delayed until now. Now, unexpectedly, it is becoming dry land. The bureau, which is responsible for construction, cannot shirk its responsibility. We have sought opinions from relevant districts and local figures and have planned to dredge. On September 10th of the 18th year, the preparatory meeting for dredging Yu Tang was opened. After repeated discussions and consultations, we unanimously elected a standing committee to be responsible for carrying out the project. The current plan of action is: First, the bureau will resurvey the siltation of the riverbed and the current state of the tributary flows and bridges to estimate the overall dredging project. Second, the bureau will assign technicians to conduct detailed surveys to determine the details of the project and establish a budget. Third, we will submit a report to the provincial government requesting approval to implement the construction steps. The steps have been decided, but the difficult problem that needs to be resolved first is how to raise the funds. Regarding the collection of dredging funds, there are methods such as apportioning the cost based on the irrigated land along the river, borrowing from the provincial treasury first and then repaying it by levying a surcharge on the land over the years, or having landowners along the river contribute money and tenants contribute labor. For example, the Wujin section of the recently dredged Tuyang Canal is funded by levying three-tenths of the busy grain transport surcharge for a period of five years. The dredging of the Zhangfu Canal in Huai'an is funded by local contributions of four-tenths, and the provincial government allocates two-tenths from disaster relief funds and designates four-tenths. These all involve referring to the first and second methods and adjusting them to the circumstances. However, the former case relates to the Grand Canal, and the latter relates to the Huai transport system. Neither is a simple matter for a single county or region, which is very different from the situation of Yu Tang. Furthermore, according to the old example of dredging Yu Tang, the general principle is to mostly adopt the third method, handling the dredging independently. Therefore, the current method of raising funds still follows the previous example in principle. However, before construction, there are fees for surveying, and before excavation, there are fees for embankment construction and bridge repair, all of which require initial expenditures. Sporadic collections may not be sufficient for the people, and apportionment by household may cause delays. It may still be necessary to use the first and second methods to borrow in advance to facilitate implementation. All of this will be determined after the actual survey is carried out and the budget is established. In short, in this time of public and private difficulty, the bureau can only do its best to strive forward.
